         <section class="body">
          <img alt="Tomato, Strawberry and Basil Gazpacho" src="http://communitytable.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/04/gazpacho-from-platter-talk1.jpg" style="display:none"/>
          <div class="figure_block feature" data-parade-clicks="false" data-parade-location-ids="featured-image" data-parade-location-types="media" data-parade-mouseovers="false" data-parade-touches="false" data-parade-type="media" data-parade-views="false">
           <figure>
            <img alt="blueberry soup recipe on platter talk_edited-2" class="addthis_shareable" data-parade-image="" data-parade-image-placeholding="" src="http://static.communitytable.parade.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/04/blueberry-soup-recipe-on-platter-talk_edited-2.jpg"/>
           </figure>
           <div class="parade-gallery-bug-container" data-parade-launch-gallery="390106">
            <div class="parade-gallery-bug" data-parade-clicks="true" data-parade-launch-gallery="390106" data-parade-location-ids="gallery-launch-bug" data-parade-location-types="promoarea" data-parade-mouseovers="false" data-parade-touches="false" data-parade-type="promoarea" data-parade-views="false">
             <div class="parade-gallery-bug-text" data-parade-launch-gallery="390106">
              Launch Gallery
             </div>
             <div class="parade-gallery-bug-meta" data-parade-launch-gallery="390106">
              13 Photos
             </div>

          <span data-parade-clicks="false" data-parade-location-ids="article" data-parade-location-types="promoarea" data-parade-mouseovers="false" data-parade-touches="false" data-parade-type="promoarea" data-parade-views="false">
           <p class="first">
            Summer often brings with it lazy afternoons by the pool, green grass, garden-fresh produce and plenty of warm sunshine. On the lunch and dinner tables it means something that is seasonally fresh, delicious, and light: The Soups of Summer. From the chilled elegance of a tomato gazpacho that is blended with basil and strawberries to a nutty and colorful summer squash soup flavored with thyme, click through the slideshow and have a taste of these
            <strong>
             13 Summer Soups That Youre Going to Love
            </strong>
            , all summer long.
           </p>

             </strong>
             , a culinary website that is all about good food, good wine, and good friends. Together with husband Scott, who is also a regular contributor to the site, the two stay busy cooking for and raising six hungry boys. The Guys from
             <strong>
              Platter Talk
             </strong>
             have been featured in a number of print and online media publications and Dan and Scott are regular guests on local food and lifestyle television programs.

		window.googletag.cmd.push( function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-728-gallery-3'); } );
	} );
}
